                                Name
                                
                                    
                                        
                                        DOF: Cooperative Comparable Rental Income  Manhattan FY 2011/2012
                                    
                                
                            

                        
                            

                                Attribution
                                
                                    
                                        
                                        Department of Finance (DOF)
                                    
                                
                            

                        
                            

                                Description
                                
                                    
                                        
                                            The Department of Finance (DOF) is required by NY State law to value condominiums or cooperatives as if they were residential rental apartment buildings.   DOF uses income information from rental p...
